Slug: kostyak
Tier: 1/5
Stats: level=1, HP~24, dmg~3
Output: static/game/monsters/undead/kostyak.webp

Generate ONE full-body or three-quarter fantasy RPG monster illustration.
Art style: Japanese anime / light novel illustration — clean line art, cel shading or soft shading, expressive silhouette, coherent anatomy for a monster or creature. Not pixel art, not photorealistic, not 3D render.
Creature name (in-game, keep recognizable vibe): «Костяк».
Monster family / type: undead / restless corpse or spirit themes.
Tier (rough threat band 1–5): 1/5.
Combat stats (for scale and menace only): level 1, HP ~24, attack power ~3. Boss encounter — larger, more imposing silhouette, dramatic presence.
Habitat / theme tags: crypt, ruins, cursed, fortress.
Design hint (RU, mood only): в бою особенно опасен быстрым ростом урона с уровнем
Background: flat solid color only, exactly #1a1025 — no gradient, no floor, no scenery, no props.
Composition: single creature centered, full figure visible within frame, readable silhouette.
Rules: no text, no letters, no watermark, no UI frame, no health bars, SFW only.
Output aspect: landscape 3:2.
